[2025-12-23T15:33:22Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: Abul Hasan Qutb Shah was the eighth and last Sultan of Golconda. He spent his formative years as a disciple of renowned Sufi saint Shah Raziuddin Hussaini Qattal, commonly known as Shah Raju. Abul Hasan married one of the daughters of Abdullah Qutb Shah, the seventh Sultan, and became Sultan after his death. Shah Raju gave Abul Hasan the nickname “X Shah” to mean “benevolent, pious king.” Aurangzeb was intent on ending the Golconda sultanate and he succeeded 14 years into Abul Hasan’s reign. Mughal propaganda then painted Abul Hasan as an incompetent, despotic, and tyrannical king. As a result of this propaganda, Abul Hasan’s nickname in Urdu and Hindi now means the opposite of its original meaning. Give X.

[2025-12-24T14:46:33Z] Kartikey Pradhan: The Hermès Kelly bag name was originally the Sac à Dépêches, or the Dispatch bag. In 1954, the costume designer for the Alfred Hitchcock film To Catch a Thief chose the bag for Grace Kelly’s character to carry. The legendary actress fell in love with the bag and kept it after the film’s release. ↵ Grace Kelly, then Princess Grace of Monaco, was later photographed carrying her bag to hide her baby bump. The photo made the cover of Life magazine. Fashionable women worldwide soon clamored for the “Kelly bag.”
